## Notes

- F1 scores range from 0.0 (worst) to 1.0 (perfect)
- Combined F1 is the average of Orientation, Adjacency, and Cycle F1 scores
- Higher priority values (1-5) indicate higher importance in optimization
- Equal priority values mean those constraints are weighted equally
